 do din ke utaar-chadhaav or manthan ke baad adwani jaise netaaon kii asahmati kii andekhi karte hue party modi ko badi or ahm bhoomika pradaan karti najar aa rahi he
 After Atal Bihari Vajpayee, Advani has been considered the leader of the tallest in the party
 rajnath ne kaha ki sabhi dal chunaavon ko chunauti ke taur par dekhte hai or bijepi ne bhi aagaamee loksabhaa chunaavon ko chunauti ke taur par sweekaar kiya he
 Modi has been entrusted with a huge responsibility only to win the elections
 rajnath ne kaha, hamen puraa vishwaas he ki congress nit upie sarkaar janata kaa bharosa kho chuki he or yah bhi bharosa he ki 2014 ke chunaavon main jitkar bijepi satta main pahonchegi
 BJP President Rajnath Singh announced the handing over of the command of the general election campaign to be held in 2014 at a press conference on the last day of the party's two-day national executive meeting
 unke saath party kii varisht netaa sushamaa swaraj, arun jetali or anant kumaar bhi maujuud the
 Rajnath told reporters, "the coming Lok Sabha election is a big challenge
 ham jeetne ja rahe hai
 Keeping in mind the election campaign, i have appointed Narendra Modi as the head of the party's campaign committee for the general election
 " Rejecting the contradictions in the BJP over Modi being given command of the campaign for the next general election, Rajnath said, "this decision has been taken with consent
 hamen puraa bharosa he ki bhaajapa hi agali sarkaar kaa netritv karegi
 " udhar, modi ko bhaajapa kii prachaar samiti kaa pramukh banaae jane se naaraaz bataae ja rahe or apane ghar ke baahar modi samarthakon ke pradarshan se 'aahat' party ke varisht netaa laalkrishna adwani ne ravivaar ko apane blog par hiltor, musolini jaise aitihaasik charitron se lekar ghayal va dhokhe ke shikaar bhishma pitamah tathaa yoddha arjuna jaise puranic charitron kaa zikr kiya
 Advani also referred to the 'dictatorial trend' on his blog, which critics see in the nature of Modi
 goa ke mukhyamantri manohar parrikar ne bhi modi kaa samarthan kiya
 He said, "you must have heard the thunderous applause
 jab isaki ghoshnaa kii gai to sabhi lagbhag paanch minute tak taaliyaan bajaate rahe
 " sushamaa swaraj, anant kumaar, raman singh (chhattisgarh ke mukhyamantri), shivaraj singh chouhan (madhya pradesh ke mukhyamantri), murali manohar joshi, arun jetali or parrikar ne bhi manch par 'bharat mata kii jai' ke naare lagaakar prachaar samiti ke adhyaksh ke rup main modi kaa swaagat kiya or unhen badhai di
 BJP workers expressed their happiness by dropping firecrackers
 bhaajapa ke purv adhyaksh em
 Venkaiah Naidu said that the committee headed by Modi will only lead the campaign, this committee will not decide the selection of candidates
 yah ek alag mudda he
 The comments madhya pradesh ke mukhyamantri shivaraj singh chouhan, jinhen adwani modi se behatar mukhyamantri bataate hai, ne bhi prachaar samiti ke adhyaksh ke rup main modi ko samarthan dene kii baat kahi
 On the other hand, Congress MP Rajiv Shukla said, "we are not scared of Modi
 ham chunavi ladaai ke liye taiyaar hai
 " khud ko badi jimmedaari milane ke baad narendra modi ne tivetor par khushi jataai
 He tweeted, Senior leaders have reposed trust in me
 ham congress mukt bharat nirmaan main koi kasar nahin chodenge
 Thanks for the support and blessings
 
 
 adwani ji se phone par baat hui, unhone mujhe apana aashirwad diya
 i am thankful to receive his blessings
 modi ko chunaav samiti kaa adhyaksh banaae jane kii ghoshnaa ke baad party kaaryakartaaon ne jamkar jashn manaanaa shuru kar diya
 According to sources, the party had directed the state units on Saturday to show a festive atmosphere in the state offices as soon as the name of Narendra Modi is announced
 is mudde ko lekar party ke varisht netaa laalkrishna adwani narendra modi ko prachaar samiti kaa sanyojak banane ke liye hami bhar chuke the, lekin modi ko is samiti kaa adhyaksh banane par adwani raji nahin bataae ja rahe the
 Advani did not attend the Goa meeting citing ill health, but according to sources, Advani was in command of the anti-modi camp, not in Goa
 prachaar samiti kaa adhyaksh banaae jane ke baad chunaav se sambandhit bijepi kii baithkon kii adhyakshata narendra modi hi karenge, lekin agar modi prachaar samiti ke sanyojak banaae jate, to chunaav ke liye hone vaale baithkon kii adhyakshata rajnath singh hi karte
 Apart from Advani, several other leaders including Jaswant Singh, Yashwant Sinha, Uma Bharati and Shatrughan Sinha also did not attend the Goa meeting
 kaha ja rahaa he ki ye netaa modi kaa kad badhane se khush nahin hai
 After two days of ups and downs, ignoring the disagreement of leaders like Advani, the party seems to be giving a big and important role to Modi
 party main atal bihari vaajapeyi ke baad duusare number par adwani ko hi sabase bade kad kaa netaa mana jaataa rahaa he
 Rajnath said that all parties see the elections as a challenge and the BJP has also accepted the upcoming Lok Sabha elections as a challenge
 chunaavon main jeet hasil karne ke makasad se hi modi ko badi jimmedaari saunpi gai he
 Rajnath said, we are very confident that the Congress-led UPA government has lost the trust of the public and is also confident that the BJP will come to power by winning the 2014 elections
 varsh 2014 main hone vaale aam chunaav ke prachaar kii kaman modi ko saunpane kii ghoshnaa bhaajapa adhyaksh rajnath singh ne party kii do divasiy rashtriya kaaryakarini kii baithak ke antim din ek samvaadadaata sammelan main kii
 He was accompanied by senior party leaders Sushma Swaraj, Arun Jaitley and Anant Kumar
 rajnath ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha, "aane vaala loksabhaa chunaav ek badi chunauti he
 We are going to win
 chunaav abhiyaan ko dhyaan main rakhte hue maine narendra modi ko aam chunaav ke liye party kii prachaar samiti kaa pramukh niyukt kiya he
 " modi ko agle aam chunaav ke liye prachaar abhiyaan kii kaman saunpe jane ko lekar bhaajapa main antarvirodhon ko khaarij karte hue rajnath ne kaha, "yah nirnay sahmati se liya gaya he
 We are confident that the BJP will lead the next government
 " On the other hand, Modi is being offended by being made the head of the bjp's campaign committee and 'hurt' by the performance of Modi supporters outside his house
 Senior party leader LK Advani on Sunday took to his blog from historical characters like Hilter, Mussolini Referring to mythological characters like Bhishma Pitamah and warrior Arjuna, who were injured and victims of deception
 adwani ne apane blog par 'taanaashaahee pravriti' kaa bhi zikr kiya, jise aalochak modi ke swabhaav main dekhte hai
 Goa Chief Minister Manohar Parrikar also supported Modi
 unhone kaha, "aapane taaliyon kii gadgadaahat suni hogi
 When it was announced, all of them continued to clap for about five minutes
 " Sushma Swaraj, Anant Kumar, Raman Singh (chief Minister of Chhattisgarh), Shivraj Singh Chauhan (chief Minister of Madhya Pradesh), Murali Manohar Joshi, Arun Jaitley and Parrikar also raised the slogan of 'bharat Mata Ki Jai' on the platform
 In form, he welcomed Modi and congratulated him
 bhaajapa kaaryakartaaon ne pataakhe chhodkar apni khushi kaa izhaar kiya

 venkaiya naidu ne kaha ki modi ke netritv vaali samiti sirf prachaar kii kaman sanbhaalegi, ummidavaaron ke chayan kaa faisla yah samiti nahin karegi

 " Party workers started celebrating fiercely after the announcement of Modi being made the chairman of the election committee

 Senior party leader LK Advani had agreed to make Narendra Modi the convener of the campaign committee on this issue, but Advani was not being persuaded to make Modi the chairman of this committee
 adwani tabiyat kharaab hone kaa hawala dete hue goa baithak main shaamil nahin hue the, lekin sutron ke mutabik adwani goa main na hokar bhi modi virdohi kheme kii kaman sanbhale hue the

 â€™â€™ Within next one or one and a half months, Board of Control for Cricket in India will announce the names of players to be included in all three grades (A, B, C) for the year 2017-18
 ummid kii ja rahi he ki is baar khilaadiyon ko board baari-bharkam salanaa selary dene ja rahaa he
 a few days ago on this issue, captain Virat Kohli met coach Vinod Rai, chairman of the administrative committee, along with coach Ravi Shastri and Mahendra Singh Dhoni
 sutron kii maane, to board khilaadiyon kii maang ko maan gaya he
 Despite this, a very serious question is arising
 baharhaal, board khilaadiyon ke vetan main kitna bhi ijapha kyon na karen, lekin sach yah he ki ve apane 'vaastavik or haq ke vetan' se milon dur hai
 If the board actually pays the players according to the terms of its constitution, then the annual salary of each player in a grade is easily at least twenty five crore rupees
 bataa den ki bisisiai apanesanvidhan ke anusaar kul salanaa rajasav kaa 70 fisadi hissaa gharelu rajya ikaayiyon or iskaa 26 fisadi hissaa khilaadiyon ko detaa he
 Out of this 26, 13 per cent of international cricketers and 10
 6 hissaa gharelu cricketron ko chalaa jaataa he

 4% of revenue is paid to junior cricketers and women players
 isi tees main se shesh chaar fisadi rajasav stadimon ke nirmaan, rakh-rakhaav or prashaskeey kharchon main chalaa jaataa he
 The formula was approved by former BCCI President Jagmohan Dalmiya in 2004 after talks with former cricketers Anil Kumble and Rahul Dravid
 lekin saal 2008 main ipel shuru hone ke baad khilaadiyon kii maangon ke saath-saath tevar bhi badal gaye
 At the same time, after the four years of IPL broadcast rights sold for about 16,000 crore rupees, the thinking of the players has gradually become more aggressive and vocal
 lekin board purv main selary ko lekar 'apana hi khel' kheltaa rahaa he
 Explain that the annual salary paid to the players is given out of the second part of the total revenue 30 percent (the first part is 70 percent), not the board's total, or 100 percent of the revenue
 vahiin, sabase ahm baat yah he ki board is 26 fisadi rajasav main bhi team india ke international maichon ke media, yaa prasaaran adhikaron (tivi, internet or mobile) se hasil hone vaali kamai ko shaamil nahin karata
 Whereas the board earns the most from broadcasting rights
 aise main ipel ke prasaaran adhikaron kii bikri se mili paise ko khilaadiyon ko die jane vaale hisse main shaamil karne kii baat hi swapnsrikhee lagati he
 Also read: That's why Virat Kohli is afraid of playing 'anything' with Pujara! vahiin, khilaadiyon ko praayojan adhikaar or isisi pratiyogitaaon se mili rakam main se bhi bahut hi maamuli hissaa miltaa he
 But now, Virat & Co
 wants the players to get a share from the board's huge revenue from broadcasting rights
 matlab bhartiya team ke prasaaran adhikaar or ipel donon ke hi prasargadhikaar se
 Please note that Star Sports has the rights to broadcast both the International Match and IPL of Team India
 bhartiya team ke maichon ke july 2012 se march 2018 tak media adhikaar (tivi, internet or mobile) ke liye star sports ne kareeb 37,00 karod rupee chukaaye the
 This brings an average of Rs 40 crore for an international match to the BCCI
 iskaa matlab yah he ki har saal sirf team india ke prasaaran adhikaar se hi bisisiai ko kareeb sava chah sau karod The money comes
 is rakam kaa 26 fisadi kareeb 160 karod rupee baithta he
 The amount spent on international players kiye jane vaala 13 fisadi yani assi karod rupee baithta he
 Now think for yourself that if this international players get only 80 crores rupees annually, then how much amount will come in the share of each player
 vahiin, aap andaja laga sakate hai ki jab bisisiai inhen prasaaran adhikaron kaa hissaa khilaadiyon ke saath nahin baant rahaa, to vah ipel ke prasaaran adhikaron se mili baari bharkam 16,000 karod rupee kii rakam ko khilaadiyon ke saath saajha karne kaa bada dil kaise dikhayega
 You see that 26 per cent of 16000 crores is 4160 crores

 This amount means that 13% of this annual 26% means that the amount spent on Team India players becomes Rs 416 crore
 sochie ki agar ye 416 karod rupee bhartiya team ke teenon gradon main shaamil khilaadiyon ko baante jaaen, to grad e main shaamil sheersh aath yaa das khilaadiyon main se prayek ke hisse main kam se kam 20 karod rupee to aaenge hi! board ke 'vaastavik samvidhan' ke anusaar is par unka puraa-puraa haq bhi banataa he! vahiin, agar isamen team india ke prasaaran adhikaar or saal main khele jane vaale maichon (prati test-15 lakh, vanade-6 lakh, tii-20-3 lakh rupee) kii fees ko ko is rakam main shaamil kar liya jaae, to yah salanaa fees kam se kam 25 karod rupee ho jaati he

 4 fisadi rajasav junior cricketron or mahila khilaadiyon ko diya jaataa he
 Of this thirty, the remaining four percent of the revenue goes towards the construction, maintenance and administrative expenses of stadiums
 is formule ko purv bisisiai adhyaksh jagmohan daalamia ne saal 2004 main purv cricketron anil kumble or rahul dravid se baatcheet ke baad hi hari jhandi dikhaai thi
 But after the IPL started in the year 2008, the attitude of the players changed as well
 vahiin haal hi main ipel ke chaar saal ke kareeb 16,000 karod rupee main bike prasaaran adhikaar ke baad khilaadiyon kii soch apane hisse ko lekar dhire-dhire or aakraamak or mukhar ho chali he
 But the board has in the past been playing its own game about salary
 bataa den ki khilaadiyon ko die jane vaala salanaa vetan kul rajasav ke duusare hisse30 fisadi (pehla hissaa 70 fisadi) main se diya jaataa he, board ke kul, yaa 100 fisadi rajasav main nahin
 At the same time, the most important thing is that the board does not include this 26 per cent of the revenue earned from Team India's international matches media, or broadcast rights (TV, Internet and mobile)
 jabaki board ko sabase zyada kamai hi prasaaran adhikaron se hoti he
 In such a situation, it seems like the dream of including the money received from the sale of broadcast rights of IPL to the players
 yah bhi padhein :isiilie viraat kohli darate hai pujaara ke saath 'kuch bhi' khilne se! At the same time, players also get a very small share from the sponsorship rights and the money received from ICC competitions
 lekin ab ab viraat and company chaahati he ki khilaadiyon ko board ko prasaaran adhikaron se hone vaali moti kamai se bhi hissaa mili
 Means both the broadcast rights of the Indian team and the broadcast rights of the IPL
 dhyaan dilaa den ki team india ke international match or ipel donon ke hi prasaaran adhikaar star sports ke paas hai
 Star Sports had paid around Rs 37,00 crore for media rights (TV, Internet and Mobile) from July 2012 to March 2018 of the Indian team's matches
 isse ek antarrashtriya match bisisiai ke liye ausat 40 karod rupee lekar aata he
 This means that every year only with the broadcasting rights of Team India, the BCCI got about six hundred and fifty million rupee aate hai
 26 per cent of this amount is about Rs 160 crore
 is rakam kaa international khilaadiyon par kharch 13 per cent to be done, that is eighty crores
 ab aap khud hi sochie ki agar sirf yahi 80 karod rupee international khilaadiyon ko salanaa mil jaaen, to har khilaadi ke hisse main kitni zyada rakam aegi
 At the same time, you can imagine that when BCCI is not sharing the share of these broadcasting rights with the players, how will it show the big heart of sharing the huge amount of 16,000 crore rupees from the IPL broadcast rights with the players
 aap dekhie ki 16000 karod kaa 26 fisadi 4160 karod rupee baithta he
 The comments yah bhi padhein :duusare din viraat kohli ne phenkaa record kaa 'satta' According to the BCCI constitution, if the amount of the right of the players is converted into annual income, then it is about Rs 832 crores (for international + domestic cricketers)
 is rakam kaa matlab yah he ki is salanaa 26 fisadi kaa 13 fisadi matlab team india ke khilaadiyon par kharch kii jane vaali rakam 416 karod rupee ho jaati he
 Think that if these 416 crores are distributed to the players of all the three grades of the Indian team, then each of the top eight or ten players in Grade a will get at least 20 crores in their share! According to the 'real constitution' of the board, they also have full rights over it! At the same time, if it includes the broadcasting rights of Team India and the fees of matches played in the year (rs
 15 lakhs, ODI-6 lakhs, T-20-3 lakhs) in this amount, then it The annual fee is at least Rs 25 crore

 Foreigners have a total deposit of Rs 96 lakh crore in Swiss banks, of which Indians have only four and a half thousand crore rupees
 in bainkon main bhartiya dwaara jamaa karai gai raashi main 2016 main takreeban 45 fisadi kii giravat ai thi jo ki kisi bhi ek saal main ai sabase badi giravat he

 april 2017 main apane halafname main chunaav sudhaaron ko lekar centre ne supreme court main kaha tha ki namakan ke vakt pratyaashee dwaara apni, apane jivan saathi or ashriton kii aay ke strot kii jaankaree jaruri karne ko centre taiyaar he
 The Center said that after much consideration it has been decided to change the rules on this issue
 jald hi iske liye notification jari kiya jayega
 Earlier, the Election Commission has also given its consent in this matter
 tippaniyan The Election Commission had said that these changes in rules are necessary for healthy democracy

 ise lekar supreme court ne centre sarkaar or chunaav ayog ko notice jari kar jawaab maanga tha
 In its affidavit, the Center has also said that it has also accepted the petitioner's statement that the statement should be taken from the candidate that he is not included in the disqualification provision under the Representation of People Act
 isse janata or riterning afasar ye jaan paaenge ki pratyaashee chunaav ladne ke yogya he yaa nahin

 centre ne kaha he ki ye policy kaa maamla he

 jiesti kii sabase kam dar 6 pratishat rakhane kaa prastaav kiya gaya he jabaki 12 or 18 pratishat kii do maanak daren hongi
